    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer2986913734070965150">Temporary. That one single word best describes my life these last few years. I’m working at a temporary job until I can finally break free. I’m my little brother’s temporary mother since our mom doesn’t give a crap about either of us. And I’m that temporary girl all the guys want to get with because I give it up so easily. According to the rumors, at least.<br/><br/>But now I’m the </span>
  <span id="freeText2986913734070965150" style="display:none">Temporary. That one single word best describes my life these last few years. I’m working at a temporary job until I can finally break free. I’m my little brother’s temporary mother since our mom doesn’t give a crap about either of us. And I’m that temporary girl all the guys want to get with because I give it up so easily. According to the rumors, at least.<br /><br />But now I’m the temporary girlfriend of Drew Callahan, college football legend and all around golden guy. He’s beautiful, sweet—and he’s hiding way more secrets than I am. He’s brought me into this fake life where everyone seems to hate me. And everyone seems to want something from him. The only thing he seems to want though is…<br /><br />Me.<br /><br />I don’t know what to believe anymore. All I know is, I think Drew needs me. And I want to be there for him.<br /><br />Forever.</span>

I felt just about every emotion possible. <br>-LOVE<br>-HATE<br>-SADNESS<br>-DISGUST<br>-HOPE<br>-FEAR<br>-HAPPINESS<br>-TURMOIL<br>Plus many many more.<br><br> If you have not read this book. READ IT! Monica Murphy is <b>An Author To Look Out For!</b><br><br><b>
  <u> One Week Girlfriend</u>

  <b>'I need help. I’m a fucking wreck and I need someone to save me before I become completely unsaved.'</b>
</i> ~Drew<br><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Used%20pt2%20for%20book%20reviews/actor-liamhemsworth_zps181ae775-1_zps1fe823d7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><i>
  <b>'He might be more trouble than he’s worth but I don’t think so. This man came into my life for some reason. Just as I came into his. Maybe we’re supposed to help each other cope. Or give each other hope.'</b>
</i> ~Fable<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Used%20pt2%20for%20book%20reviews/actress-elisha_cuthbert_01_zps3ea253d9-1_zps04b3d2c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405255i/789220.jpg" alt=" photo actress-elisha_cuthbert_01_zps3ea253d9-1_zps04b3d2c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Home for the Holiday's</b><br>Schools are letting out for Thanksgiving break but home is the last place 21yr old Drew wants to be. His childhood home is more like the house of horrors. He knows he can't face going there alone so he decides to take his girlfriend with him. Problem is he does not have a girlfriend.<br><br><b>Making Ends Meet. Well, That's the plan</b><br>Fable works two jobs to help pay the bills. Looking after her little brother mind as well be another full time job. At 13 he is starting to get in to trouble at school. With a mother who could care less, Fable must now play the role of responsible adult instead of attending college and partying like other young adults her age.<br><br><b>Ummm... Could you be my girlfriend?</b><br>Drew waits outside of a local bar called La Salle for Fable to get off work. When she finally does he approaches her. A few words are exchanged before he can ask what he really wants..<br><br><b>“I want you to pretend to be my girlfriend for a week.”</b> ~Drew<br><br>Fable cannot understand why Drew Callahan "the golden boy quarterback" needs her, when he can have any girl he wants. But deep inside she knows why. Fable has a rep. She is considered easy and even admits to Drew that she has hooked up with a few of his teammates. <br><br>Fable is reluctant at first but once he tells her $3,000.00 is what he'll pay. And assures her sex is not involved, her answer is an automatic YES. Her family needs the money she can't turn it down plain and simple.<br><br><b>Welcome to the Twilight Zone</b><br>It takes Fable<b> 1.5</b> seconds to realize that everything is not what it seems. The picture perfect life Drew has is a facade and in reality is not all it's cracked up to be. In fact as the week goes on she realizes that something is wrong. And she is afraid of what may have Drew so on edge in his own home.<br><br><u>My Thoughts -SPOILER FREE</u><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Used%20pt2%20for%20book%20reviews/wtfwordpic_zps526719e3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br> YES, WHAT THE FUCK? That was my first thought as the story unfolded and I realized what was going on. I had to pause...<br> <br><br>The deeper into the plot the more I became enraged.<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Used%20pt2%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_m8ytyidIsB1rnudxp_zpsbf67e57c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I thought.. Why? How? Why? How? On constant repeat.<br>Then Suddenly...<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/EMOTIONAL%20WORD%20GIFS%20PT2/quoteofhate_zps51f6eca6-1_zpsc23d200c-1_zps307a61c6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/516582230" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/516582230?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17903637-one-week-girlfriend">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=na">na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer516582230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8920925685476012529"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br/><br/><br/><b>He might be more trouble than he's worth but I don't think so. This man came into my life for some reason. Just as I came into his. Maybe we're supposed to help each other cope. Or give each other hope.</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/dde7b8601d52b6a57179dbe61870261d_zpsefrkewsw.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431485235i/14840606._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo dde7b8601d52b6a57179dbe61870261d_zpsefrkewsw.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Drew Callahan and Fable Maguire come from two different worlds and yet they seem to have so much in common. Drew is the popular college football player and Fable is a waitress at the local bar in town that all the college kids hang out as. She's got quite the reputation aro</span>
  <span id="freeText8920925685476012529" style="display:none"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br><br><br><b>He might be more trouble than he's worth but I don't think so. This man came into my life for some reason. Just as I came into his. Maybe we're supposed to help each other cope. Or give each other hope.</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/dde7b8601d52b6a57179dbe61870261d_zpsefrkewsw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431485235i/14840606._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo dde7b8601d52b6a57179dbe61870261d_zpsefrkewsw.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Drew Callahan and Fable Maguire come from two different worlds and yet they seem to have so much in common. Drew is the popular college football player and Fable is a waitress at the local bar in town that all the college kids hang out as. She's got quite the reputation around campus, and she doesn't even attend the school. Fable's home life is less than perfect. She works two jobs to support her and her younger brother, while her mother goes out and drinks and sleeps around with different men. Fable turns to guys for affection. Always searching for that closeness to make her feel the love she clearly never received at home. Her reputation is also exaggerated just a tad!! Drew's family life is beyond heartbreaking and dysfunctional. He goes through life trying to avoid the guilt and shame of his past. Football and school are his escape. <br><br><br><br>Now Drew is faced with a dilemma. He's being forced to go home for Thanksgiving week and he decides to approach Fable, who he has never spoken to, and asks if she will come home with him and pretend to be his girlfriend for the week. He offers her $3000 for her time. At first things are awkward since they hardly know each other but as they spend time together, feelings are clearly starting to develop between them.<br><br><br><br><br>I have to say this story was very predictable to me. I knew right away what was haunting Drew and that huge reveal at the end?? I saw that coming a mile away. Although I think that someone is telling a huge lie!! <b>BUT</b>, even though it was predictable, I really did enjoy this story so much! I loved how at times some of the writing was very poetic. I also found myself falling for Drew. <br><br><br><br><br>These two have some scorching hot chemistry and I am so happy that I decided to read this when all the books have already been released because that cliffy at the end has me dying to get to book two as soon as I can!!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8920925685476012529" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505391509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8735570028608456462"><b>4+ SWEET AS M-A-R-S-H-M-A-L-L-O-W STARS.</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"We'll settle back into our usual roles. where you hate me and I hate you. It'll be a lie. I might've hated you before all this, but now... I think I'm falling in love with you."</b>
</i> <br/><br/><b>Drew --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792876i/569623._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Fable --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405000i/788498._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Drew Callahan</b> is going home for Thanksgiving and he needs a fake girlfriend for a week to bring to his parents' house. That way, he can show them that he is in fact capable of keeping a girl for a longer amount of time, and he hopes this way his father and stepm</span>
  <span id="freeText8735570028608456462" style="display:none"><b>4+ SWEET AS M-A-R-S-H-M-A-L-L-O-W STARS.</b><br><br><i>
  <b>"We'll settle back into our usual roles. where you hate me and I hate you. It'll be a lie. I might've hated you before all this, but now... I think I'm falling in love with you."</b>
</i> <br><br><b>Drew --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792876i/569623._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fable --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405000i/788498._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Drew Callahan</b> is going home for Thanksgiving and he needs a fake girlfriend for a week to bring to his parents' house. That way, he can show them that he is in fact capable of keeping a girl for a longer amount of time, and he hopes this way his father and stepmother won't bother him too much while he's at home. But that's not the only reason why he's so dreadful of going back to the place where he grew up.<br><br><b>"I need a buffer to get me through what could end up being one of the worst weeks of my life. Thank God for Fable. She has no clue how much she's helping me. She can never know either." ~ Drew</b><br><br><b>Fable Maguire</b> has always been everybody's second choice. No one really seems to care about her. She's from the "poorer" side of town so she has to work extra hours to keep up with paying rent and taking care of her little brother, since their mother's almost never home. So, when Drew Callahan, the university's golden boy and star quarterback offers her 3000 dollars to be his fake girlfriend for a week, Fable decides that even though it makes her feel cheap and used, that amount of much needed money, makes Drew's offer one she can't refuse.<br><br><b>"There is no room for romance in my life. It's so stupid, but I let guys use me because for one fleeting moment, when he's focusing all of his attention on me and no one else, it feels good. It helps me forget that no one really cares." ~ Fable.</b><br><br>What neither of them expects though, is that although their relationship is based on "appearances", slowly but surely they begin to rely on each other more and more. They realize that they're not so different from each other, that they're both broken deep down inside and that maybe their "temporary" relationship can become something much more permanent.<br><br><b>"This man came into my life for some reason. Just as I came into his. Maybe we're supposed to help each other cope. Or give each other hope." ~ Fable</b> <br><br>But their time together isn't filled with moments of bliss alone... dark secrets from Drew's past threaten to ruin their already fragile relationship. Then there's the fact that neither of them is fully sure of the other one's feelings, they're both unsure whether the other one's feelings are real are just part of the act, part of the "fake" relationship they've gotten their selves into.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Everything between us isn't real and I have to remember that. No matter how good it feels."</b>
</i><br><br><br>And then there's the <b><u>STEPMOTHER FROM HELL</u> : Adele...</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/433302.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p>Seriously, about halfway through the story she was already getting on my nerves and I just wanted her to <i>leave</i> them alone!<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/454589.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p>And just when things couldn't get any worse, she had to OFF COURSE make me HATE her even more with this line : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["Vanessa's not your sister, Andrew." Adele pauses, the smile she shoots my direction devastating. "She was your daughter." <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405000ra/788499.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><b>That was just BEYOND messed up!!!!!</b><br><br>And then, the ending. Don't expect it to be a happy one... Drew did some things that made me a little angry.<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405000ra/788500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p> But Drew, I understand why you did it and I forgive you and I just want you to be happy because<p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/535470.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>And to be honest, the ending gave me hope in a way too...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Because of the MARSHMALLOW-message in Drew's letter <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><b>"Like souls find each other, you know. As corny as it sounds, I'm starting to believe we were brought together for a reason." ~ Fable</b><br><br><br><b>One Week Girlfriend</b> was a very surprising, unputdownable, fast-paced story that I very much enjoyed reading. Thankfully, the sequel is out already, so I'll be moving on to the second part of Drew and Fable story in <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17316075.Second_Chance_Boyfriend__Drew___Fable___2_" title="Second Chance Boyfriend (Drew + Fable, #2) by Monica Murphy" rel="nofollow noopener">Second Chance Boyfriend</a></b> right away. I already know I'll be keeping my *fingers crossed* for a happy ending for these two... <br><br><br>****<br><br></p></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7506398241514430313"><b>4.5 MARSHMALLOW (but not the soft and squishy marshmallows….no, these are the fucked-up marshmallows!!!) STARS!!!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1283.photobucket.com/user/jennifer_butler2/media/Shock/nickiblink_zps68f9bbb9.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>I did not expect to enjoy this book so much! The blurb sounded predictable and cliché (guy asks girl to be his pretend girlfriend…boring, right?...WRONG!). I found myself smiling and swooning and gasping and cursing….a lot!!! <br/><br/><b>My Drew:</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386524700i/7383472._SY540_.jpg' alt='.' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>My Fable:</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386524700i/7383473._SY540_.jpg' alt='Candice Accola - candice-accola Photo' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Drew is a gorgeous all-star in college. Fable is the small-town slut. Drew convinces Fable to be his pretend girlfriend for a week over th</span>
  <span id="freeText7506398241514430313" style="display:none"><b>4.5 MARSHMALLOW (but not the soft and squishy marshmallows….no, these are the fucked-up marshmallows!!!) STARS!!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1283.photobucket.com/user/jennifer_butler2/media/Shock/nickiblink_zps68f9bbb9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388434821ra/7834389.gif" alt=" photo nickiblink_zps68f9bbb9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I did not expect to enjoy this book so much! The blurb sounded predictable and cliché (guy asks girl to be his pretend girlfriend…boring, right?...WRONG!). I found myself smiling and swooning and gasping and cursing….a lot!!! <br><br><b>My Drew:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386524700i/7383472._SY540_.jpg" alt="." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Fable:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386524700i/7383473._SY540_.jpg" alt="Candice Accola - candice-accola Photo" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew is a gorgeous all-star in college. Fable is the small-town slut. Drew convinces Fable to be his pretend girlfriend for a week over the holidays. He has an aversion to most girls, but Fable seems to get under his skin…in a good way. When they get to Drew’s parent’s house, Fable quickly realizes that his family is not so perfect. Drew and Fable grow closer together through the shit storm that is Drew’s family. I can’t say much more without spoiling.<br><br>The writing is not cliché.<br><br>The characters are not cliché. <br><br>The story is definitely not cliché.<br><br>I love Drew. I love Fable. Excited to read the next one!<br></span>

<div id="review_503588628" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503588628" />
    <a title="Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9164629-amy-j-romance-author-reader-events"><img alt="Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575841970p2/9164629.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503588628?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events" href="/user/show/9164629-amy-j-romance-author-reader-events">Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">ANGSTY LOVERS</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events by: </span>
      Becky N
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9164629-amy-j-romance-author-reader-events?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503588628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12784848100883316254">Every now and then I pick a book listed in the news feed on the home page and immediately read it. A blogger had just reviewed this book and I thought , hmmm I love the cover and she said it had angst...SOLD!<br/><br/><b>MARSHMALLOW!!!</b><br/><br/>I love it, and to know what I am referring to you must read the book.<br/> <br/>The premise of the story doesn't seem to be too unique upon first glance, but its exactly what the title implies and yet is soooo much more and better. I did not expect to find such emotion and even some angs</span>
  <span id="freeText12784848100883316254" style="display:none">Every now and then I pick a book listed in the news feed on the home page and immediately read it. A blogger had just reviewed this book and I thought , hmmm I love the cover and she said it had angst...SOLD!<br><br><b>MARSHMALLOW!!!</b><br><br>I love it, and to know what I am referring to you must read the book.<br> <br>The premise of the story doesn't seem to be too unique upon first glance, but its exactly what the title implies and yet is soooo much more and better. I did not expect to find such emotion and even some angst in this story but was pleasantly surprised when I did. The story is told from alternating POV's which quite honestly I don't normally like, but in this story it is done perfectly. The reader is continually drawn into what the other character is thinking due to the deep and emotional story lines taking place. Thats right there are real true deep back stories in this book, but I can't tell you what they are due to spoilers. Just <b> TRUST</b> me on this. <br><br>Fable is the lead female character and yes her name is quite <br>distracting but fitting. She is strong and not a whining virgin. I love that she is sassy with a backbone. I love that she is the one that is strong over the big hunky jock that is Drew Callahan. So unexpected. <br><br>SWOONWORTHY DREW is HOTTTT! Not only is he hot he is deep. A fine ass football jock with.... baggage, lots and lots of baggage. He is so surprised by Fable and all that she can give him its touching. Not many young male lead characters grasp the need for this. My favorite sceene....under the trellis. SIGHHHHH! <br><br>The back and forth is typical as they get to know each other and reveal their insecurities. Typical but I loved every single moment. <br>Great job Monica Murphy!<br>P.S.<br>Adele can SUCK IT! I hope she gets hers in book two<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/gif/skez520mia/SEXY%20GIFS/gifheadscratchZer0.gif?o=53" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398094ra/768969.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12784848100883316254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/505745586?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505745586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7702149207510272866"><b>4 1/2 Marshmallow Stars!!</b> <br/><br/>Drew is a quiet, hot, rich, college quarterback who offers townie/barmaid Fable, (yes, that’s her name love it right!) three thousand dollars to spend Thanksgiving week with him and his dysfunctional parents, posing as his girlfriend. <br/><br/>What would a handsome guy like Drew need a pretend girlfriend for? <br/><br/>It’s pretty obvious that Drew has some really dark secrets. I would say that the majority of readers will be able to figure his secrets out but that’s not the allure of the</span>
  <span id="freeText7702149207510272866" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 Marshmallow Stars!!</b> <br><br>Drew is a quiet, hot, rich, college quarterback who offers townie/barmaid Fable, (yes, that’s her name love it right!) three thousand dollars to spend Thanksgiving week with him and his dysfunctional parents, posing as his girlfriend. <br><br>What would a handsome guy like Drew need a pretend girlfriend for? <br><br>It’s pretty obvious that Drew has some really dark secrets. I would say that the majority of readers will be able to figure his secrets out but that’s not the allure of the story…Fable tries to save Drew from his demons and they fall in love through this charade.<br> <br>Fable is a terrific character! She is outspoken, beautiful, loyal she has been searching for someone/anyone to love and make her feel. She has her own baggage but together they make the perfect couple. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399676ra/773725.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”Honestly, I don’t quite know how we got to this point. I hated him on sight. I did this only for the money. I thought he was a fucked up mess. I still think he’s a fucked up mess. But so am I. And he’s so beautiful, so thoughtful, so vulnerable. We can be a mess together. I want to heal him. I know I can heal him.”</i>
</b><br><br>Fable’s week in this beautiful guest house on the water is like a fairytale in a way. Please note that the role of evil stepmother will be played by…Adele. Yep the woman is EVIL!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405050i/788615.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Fable and Drew’s relationship develops and grows beautifully despite his issues. The couple has great chemistry and they both find someone to rely on and trust. When the week is over their lives will never be the same. <br> <br>The ending leaves us with a "hopeful" cliffhanger.<br></span>

<div id="review_524278886" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524278886" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524278886?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tortured-abused-hero">tortured-abused-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524278886" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13303518412687300920"><br/>This was like taking a step into the unknown for me. I don’t read a huge amount of New Adult romances, I’m mostly an erotica gal, but something about the synopsis of this one really appealed to me and I decided to give it a go and I’m so glad I did. It’s a highly accomplished debut novel and I devoured it in one sitting. It’s intriguing, fascinating, sad and very compelling and has a real Pretty Woman vibe going on.<br/><br/>Drew is our hero – all American college football star, born with a whole silver d</span>
  <span id="freeText13303518412687300920" style="display:none"><br />This was like taking a step into the unknown for me. I don’t read a huge amount of New Adult romances, I’m mostly an erotica gal, but something about the synopsis of this one really appealed to me and I decided to give it a go and I’m so glad I did. It’s a highly accomplished debut novel and I devoured it in one sitting. It’s intriguing, fascinating, sad and very compelling and has a real Pretty Woman vibe going on.<br /><br />Drew is our hero – all American college football star, born with a whole silver dinner service in his mouth. A highly privileged childhood with his Father and Step-Mother but it seems money doesn’t buy happiness and right from the getgo Drew’s bone-deep sadness and extreme vulnerability were there in full force. I really felt for him – at first, I had absolutely no clue what was driving this guy to deceive his family that he had a girlfriend and, even as I guessed some of it, nothing would have prepared me for the whole shocking truth.<br /><br />So he decides to hire Fable to be his one week girlfriend to take home to his wealthy family to spend Thanksgiving with them. Fable is most definitely from the wrong side of the tracks and, due to her loser and often absent mother, has taken on whole responsibility for raising her wayward thirteen year old brother. She works in a bar and also as a waitress and has a bit of a reputation amongst the college jocks for being easy and so Drew decides she’s the one for the job.<br /><br />He’s wealthy enough to offer her a sizeable sum of money to make a big difference to her and her brother’s lives – he must really need to convince his family he’s dating. At first, I wondered if he was gay but his obvious attraction for Fable convinced me otherwise.<br /><br />I really liked Fable. For a young girl, she’s a wise old soul and she’s very intuitive and soon begins to see that not everything in the garden is rosy at Drew’s family home. She guesses part of the dark and terrible secret, the motivations behind Drew’s actions but she and Drew do not know it all and there is more shocking revelations to come.<br /><br />It was so lovely to see how these two travelled the road not yet taken – two kids from totally opposite backgrounds finding something in common and solace in one another's arms. Drew is damaged with a capital D and he’s putting is life on hold dealing with his issues, not really living at all, but Fable sets something free in him and she comforts him on a level that he’s just not been able to find before. Fable also lacks in self-worth and I wish I could say that Drew helped her there but he’s a little too wrapped up in his own issues but there is potential for more as the story is not yet complete and with a bit of a cliffhanger, we are left hanging on for more.<br /><br />4 stars New Adult Romance<br /><br /><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13303518412687300920" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_505445801" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/505445801" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/505445801?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505445801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11715636482621822686"><b>This man came into my life for some reason. Just as I came into his. Maybe we’re supposed to help each other cope. Or give each other hope.</b><br/><br/>Drew Callahan is a college football star. He appears to have the perfect life. He’s a good looking guy, a good student, a great football player. He seems to have it all together, but it is all a facade. <br/><b>
  <i> From the outside, my family looks perfect. Well, as perfect as a family can be with one dead mother, and one dead sister. A fucked up stepmother and a col</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText11715636482621822686" style="display:none"><b>This man came into my life for some reason. Just as I came into his. Maybe we’re supposed to help each other cope. Or give each other hope.</b><br><br>Drew Callahan is a college football star. He appears to have the perfect life. He’s a good looking guy, a good student, a great football player. He seems to have it all together, but it is all a facade. <br><b>
  <i> From the outside, my family looks perfect. Well, as perfect as a family can be with one dead mother, and one dead sister. A fucked up stepmother and a cold as hell father. Yeah. Real perfect.</i>
</b><br><br>Drew has to go home for Thanksgiving. Something he really doesn’t want to do. He’s not sure he can handle it alone. So he decides to bring someone with him... Fable. <br><br>Fable is a local in the college town Drew lives in. Her life is totally different from Drew’s. She can’t go to college. No time or money. She works two jobs to help support her younger brother. Fable has a bit of a reputation from working at the local bar, and 'hooking up' with some of Drew's team mates.<br><b>
  <i>It’s so stupid, but I let guys use me because for that one fleeting moment, when he’s focusing all of his attention on me and no one else, it feels good. It helps me forget that no one really cares.</i>
</b><br><br>Drew decides she would make the perfect candidate for his one-week, temporary girlfriend. When Drew approaches Fable, she has no idea why he would need her help. Drew should have no problem bringing home a real girlfriend. That has never been the problem for Drew. Girls always want to date him. But he can't do it. He has his reasons, which is why he needs Fable. She is hesitant at first, but when Drew offers her $3,000 for the week, she can’t turn it down. She needs the money to support her family. <br><br>After spending some time together at Drew’s home, Fable can immediately tell something is up. Drew has something from his past he is hiding. Something no one can ever find out about. The guilt eats at him. He doesn't feel like he can tell anyone. <br><b>
  <i> “If I told you the truth, you’d hate me.” His voice is harsh, his expression pained. “I hate me for what I’ve done.”</i>
</b><br><br>I figured out part of the big twist pretty early on, but then there is something else that comes to light...<br><br>I really enjoyed this one. It wasn’t as light and fluffy as I thought it would be. Fable was a great leading lady. She is tough and I love how she helped Drew with everything. And Drew- Loved him! Hated what he had to go through, my heart broke for him. Hopefully in book 2 he can learn to forgive himself. The chemistry between Drew and Fable was hot! The ending was a bit of a cliffhanger, but the note- <b>M-A-R-S-H-M-A-L-L-O-W... </b>gives me hope for a HEA in book 2 for these two! <br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/marshmallow/hi41_2009/Marshmallow.jpg?o=72" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405009i/788528.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Some of my favorite quotes...<br><br><b>
  <i>I need help. I’m a fucking wreck and I need someone to save me before I become completely unsaved. -Drew<br><br>I thought he was a fucked up mess. I still think he’s a fucked up mess. But so am I. And he’s so beautiful, so thoughtful, so vulnerable. We can be a mess together. I want to heal him. -Fable<br><br>“There’s no going back,” he whispers, as if he can read my mind. I slowly nod, too overcome to find words.<br>“Once I’m inside you, you’re mine. I want you to be mine, Fable.”<br>“I want to be yours. I want to belong to you, Drew. Only you.”<br><br>I always want him. Always. It’s always been like this between us, too. We come together and we simply... combust. So easily. Beautifully. -Fable</i>
</b><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5665183221576946333"><br/><b>M</b>eet Drew, football player, hottie, has money so what more could he want? Well right now he needs.... <br/><br/><b>A</b> girlfriend for 1 week. Take her home for fall break to<br/><br/><b>R</b>un interference between him and his dad and stepmom! And he is willing to pay for it!<br/><br/><b>S</b>o it wasn't an offer Fable, a struggling waitress trying to make ends meet while taking care of <br/><br/><b>H</b>er brother and alcoholic mom could refuse. She didn't ask questions. Get her $3K, play nice for a week and be done! <br/><br/><b>M</b>aybe he had secrets, maybe he was gay, ma</span>
  <span id="freeText5665183221576946333" style="display:none"><br /><b>M</b>eet Drew, football player, hottie, has money so what more could he want? Well right now he needs.... <br /><br /><b>A</b> girlfriend for 1 week. Take her home for fall break to<br /><br /><b>R</b>un interference between him and his dad and stepmom! And he is willing to pay for it!<br /><br /><b>S</b>o it wasn't an offer Fable, a struggling waitress trying to make ends meet while taking care of <br /><br /><b>H</b>er brother and alcoholic mom could refuse. She didn't ask questions. Get her $3K, play nice for a week and be done! <br /><br /><b>M</b>aybe he had secrets, maybe he was gay, maybe he just hated his parents.... Fable didn't know and honestly <br /><br /><b>A</b>ll she cared about what getting the money. The <br /><br /><b>L</b>ast thing either one of them expected was to fall for each other. <br /><br /><b>L</b>ove or lust, it didn't matter because <br /><br /><b>O</b>nce Fable knew the truth about his secrets, Drew knew he would lose her. Drew could barely deal with the secret himself? <br /><br /><b>W</b>hy would he do that to someone else? <br /><br /><blockquote>"I want to be yours," I answer in a breathy whisper. "I want to belong to you, Drew. Only you."</blockquote><br /><br />I loved this book. It sounds so cheesy to say this but it consumed me. I couldn't put it down and when I had no other choice, I found myself thinking about it constantly until I could get back to reading. I need the sequel like yesterday! I have got to know what happens and I so hope these 2 don't disappoint me. I want them to have their "happy ever after." They both deserve it!</span>

<div id="review_662523950" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/662523950" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/662523950?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer662523950" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7842069042313902443"><b>One Week Girlfriend</b> knocked me off my feet! I totally fell in love with this emotional and heart-wrenching story! <br/><br/>Drew pays Fable to be his fake girlfriend for the week of Thanksgiving, a week he must spend at home. He needs Fable for protection but as a reader you don’t know why. Fable agrees because she can barely make ends meet working as a barmaid. She needs the money. She has a poor excuse of a mother, and a teenage brother to take care of. She knows Drew made this proposition because she h</span>
  <span id="freeText7842069042313902443" style="display:none"><b>One Week Girlfriend</b> knocked me off my feet! I totally fell in love with this emotional and heart-wrenching story! <br /><br />Drew pays Fable to be his fake girlfriend for the week of Thanksgiving, a week he must spend at home. He needs Fable for protection but as a reader you don’t know why. Fable agrees because she can barely make ends meet working as a barmaid. She needs the money. She has a poor excuse of a mother, and a teenage brother to take care of. She knows Drew made this proposition because she has a reputation of being easy, a reputation she doesn’t fight, but it’s not deserved, and it cuts her that this is the reason he’s picked her. She’s seen Drew at the bar before with his college mates and knows his type, entitled and used to getting what he wants, girls being no exception. Or so she thinks. <br /><br />Turns out Drew and Fable both have preconceived ideas about each other that are very wrong. Spending the week together they slowly realize this and begin to lean on each other, confide in one another, and connect emotionally:<br /><b>
  <i><br />Drew reaches out and grabs hold of my hand again and when I look up at him, he smiles at me in the darkness. I have this sudden sense that it’s the two of us against the world.<br /></i>
</b><br />Mental and emotional connections are always so much more powerful than physical ones, IMO, but with Drew and Fable they have it all:<br /><b>
  <i><br />We’re only two days into this fake relationship crap and this is where we’re at, wrapped around each other like pretzels and hoping like hell we don’t have to let go of each other any time soon.—Drew<br /></i>
</b><br />One thing they don’t have going for them is the demons that Drew has to fight. Trust me when I say they are ugly and fill me with murderous thoughts!! It won’t take you long to put two and two together to figure out what happened, but it will stun you and make you sick for poor Drew! Fable realizes that something really awful has happened to him to damage him so, and she’s determined to stick by his side and help him through. <br /><br />Monica Murphy managed to write a story made me swoon, ache and enrage me at the same time!! It’s one of those reads you don’t want to put down! And, oh, that ending! It’s not a cliff but it’s definitely NOT where I want things to end. I’m writing this itching to click over to purchase and load <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17316075.Second_Chance_Boyfriend__Drew___Fable___2_" title="Second Chance Boyfriend (Drew + Fable, #2) by Monica Murphy" rel="nofollow noopener">Second Chance Boyfriend</a> so I can get my Drew and Fable HEA! *runs off to buy* <br /><br />Favorite Quotes (these are spoilers):<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /> <b><i><br />“This isn’t a game to me, Fable. This is my life. And I want you to be a part of it. But if you’d rather f&amp;%k around with other guys, then I can’t deal with that. I want you and you only. I’m not sharing you with anyone else. “<br /><br />I’ve always thought of myself as an independent person. I belong to no one. But the idea of belonging to Drew fills me with so much joy, I’m afraid I might burst. <br />“I want you to be mine, Fable.”<br />Loosening his hold on my wrists, he dips his head, nuzzling my cheek, my nose. It’s the sweetest, sexiest gesture and I moan as I circle my arms around his neck and cradle him close. <br />“I want to be yours,” I answer in a breathy whisper. “I want to belong to you, Drew. Only you.”<br /></i></b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7842069042313902443" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6132793463514152022">"The course of true love never did run smooth" - William Shakespeare.<br/><br/>I can't quite comprehend how the author managed to fit so much into this short emotional read. Full of secrets and heartache this is so much more than just a story of love, more like a journey of two lost hearts.<br/><br/>From the start I knew that I would love Fable the relationship with her younger brother and the life she finds herself in shows a strength and courage, she is so likeable and genuine everything in me wanted her to have </span>
  <span id="freeText6132793463514152022" style="display:none">"The course of true love never did run smooth" - William Shakespeare.<br /><br />I can't quite comprehend how the author managed to fit so much into this short emotional read. Full of secrets and heartache this is so much more than just a story of love, more like a journey of two lost hearts.<br /><br />From the start I knew that I would love Fable the relationship with her younger brother and the life she finds herself in shows a strength and courage, she is so likeable and genuine everything in me wanted her to have her long awaited HEA.<br /><br />The author leads you right into the darkness that surrounds drew the main male lead in the story and instantly the story grabbed me waiting for the HEA from chapter one. Drew is surprisingly vulnerable from the start, my Heart broke learning more of his story.<br /><br />This story was witty, charming and unputdownable, it also leaves the door wide open for book two.<br /><br />"Alive. Cherished. Loved."<br /><br />4 marshmallow Stars.<br /><br />Ps I think I need a light read now please.</span>

I can’t let her think this is over between us.<br><br>She still keeps her face averted, as if she’s afraid to look me in the eyes. “It’s too late. There’s nothing you can do. It’s o—over between us.”<br><br>I remove my hand from the wall to cup her cheek, forcing her to look at me. Those big, scared eyes meet mine and for a moment I’m lost. Like we’re back in time and at my parents’ guesthouse when we were about to embark on something big. Something serious. I had this girl in the palm of my hand and she had me. But I was such a chicken shit, I let her slip right out of my grip and now look at her.She’s…different. Her entire life has changed in a matter of weeks. And I had nothing to do with it. She’s moved on while I’m still stuck.<br><br>The realization is staggering.<br><br>“I need to get back to work,” she whispers. “You should go back to your friends.”I stroke her face, let my fingers trace the delicate line of her jaw. She closes her eyes, I notice the delicate movement of her throat as she swallows and I dip my head, this time making that connection I so desperately want. My mouth on hers, breathing her breath, tasting her lips, the sweet, mysterious depths within. She parts her lips immediately and I take advantage, slipping my tongue inside, tangling it with hers.<br><br>A groan escapes me and she breaks the kiss first, our eyes opening at the same time and we stare at each other without saying a word, her gaze dropping to my mouth again. I know it.<br><br>“Fable. Everything okay?”We both turn our heads to see some guy standing a few feet away, big and intimidating, dressed all in black, his gaze sharp as it lingers on me. He looks like he wants to kick my ass.Great. After his interruption, the feeling’s mutual.<br><br>“I’m fine. Just getting back to work.” She shoves at me and I step back, letting her escape. Just like that.<br><br>Fable doesn’t look at me as she heads into the restaurant. <br>Doesn’t say a word to me or the guy and we’re left outside alone, glaring at each other, sizing each other up. Bet she makes more money too. <br><br>“I’m her boyfriend.”He lifts his brows, a little chuckle escaping him. “Really? Funny, she didn’t mention you when we were together last night.”<br><br>I’m so fucking shocked by what the asshole says that by the time I find my voice, he’s gone.</i>

<span id="freeTextContainer8723042931641657229"><b>4 FLUFFY MARSHMALLOW SHAPED STARS!</b><br/><br/>I couldn't help rounding this debut novel up to four stars, simply because of the steam factor and the over-the-top angst and drama. So, here's what I pictured:<br/><br/><b>Drew --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792367._SY540_.jpg' width='266' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He's considered the rich, golden boy, but he has skeletons in his closet, and demons that haunt him. He <i>needs</i> Fable more than he thinks. <br/><br/><b>& Fable -- </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792368._SY540_.jpg' width='266' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>She's the "town slut" - but not really. She feels empty and lost and tired all the time, but she's strong & beautiful. Maybe Fable & Drew will fill eac</span>
  <span id="freeText8723042931641657229" style="display:none"><b>4 FLUFFY MARSHMALLOW SHAPED STARS!</b><br><br>I couldn't help rounding this debut novel up to four stars, simply because of the steam factor and the over-the-top angst and drama. So, here's what I pictured:<br><br><b>Drew --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792367._SY540_.jpg" width="266" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's considered the rich, golden boy, but he has skeletons in his closet, and demons that haunt him. He <i>needs</i> Fable more than he thinks. <br><br><b>&amp; Fable -- </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792368._SY540_.jpg" width="266" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's the "town slut" - but not really. She feels empty and lost and tired all the time, but she's strong &amp; beautiful. Maybe Fable &amp; Drew will fill each others' emptiness. Maybe Drew will appreciate her. <br><br><b>Their steamy make-out sessions --</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406239ra/792369.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Again, but in the shower -- </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792370._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The cute bits --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792371.jpg" width="500" height="290" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The angry bits --</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406239ra/792372.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The sad bits -- </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406239ra/792373.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>But wait, there's hope --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792374.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406239i/792375.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cutest code word. Ever. And that letter... <br><br>***<br><br>OVERALL: <br><br>- I was impressed with the story for a debut novel! <br>- The steam factor = turned ON &amp; UP. <br>- I figured out the "twist" earlier on in the story, but still, when everything was revealed, I was no less repulsed, angry, and shaking with rage. <br>- Intense, over-the-top drama with a lot of angst, while taking "family dysfunction" to whole 'nother level. <br>- Finished in one setting, two and a half hours, tops. <br>- I'm actually really looking forward the sequel! Drew better WORK to get Fable back! <br>- Finally, I really liked Fable's relationship with her little brother, Owen. Very realistic, natural, and sweet :)<br><br>***<br><br>Happy readings!</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/591757552?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591757552" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10550089144905807587">I buddy read this book with Elena :]<br/><br/>I should have read this ages ago. The writing style is really good and easy to read, and the romance is as fluffy as marshmallows. Marshmallow cuteness! If you're looking for a go - to NA book, give this one a try. <br/><br/><b>Drew Callahan</b>, a rich, attractive football player hired <b>Fable Maguire</b> to be his one week girlfriend for Thanksgiving. Fable is the breadwinner of her family and takes the opportunity since her mom can't do a better job and she wants to provide a goo</span>
  <span id="freeText10550089144905807587" style="display:none">I buddy read this book with Elena :]<br /><br />I should have read this ages ago. The writing style is really good and easy to read, and the romance is as fluffy as marshmallows. Marshmallow cuteness! If you're looking for a go - to NA book, give this one a try. <br /><br /><b>Drew Callahan</b>, a rich, attractive football player hired <b>Fable Maguire</b> to be his one week girlfriend for Thanksgiving. Fable is the breadwinner of her family and takes the opportunity since her mom can't do a better job and she wants to provide a good life for her little brother. Drew knows that his family wouldn't like her because she has a bad reputation but there's <i>more</i> to that and Fable sensed Drew is hiding a deep, dark secret that makes him imperfect.<br /><br />The plot twist is predictable. Though I made the right guess about Drew's secret, my heart still cracks a little for him [I loathe her step-mother with burning passion]. I love how Fable comforts him through his difficult times. She's caring and straightforward. I just adore these two characters and I'm continuing this series. <br /><br />More Marshmallows :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="10550089144905807587" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Syndi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1656405-syndi"><img alt="Syndi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560317991p2/1656405.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3447231686?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Syndi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Syndi" href="/user/show/1656405-syndi">Syndi</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3447231686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10061727962833176863">I do not like this book. <br/><br/>It is good that the author brings out the issue of child molestation to surface. However she did not give enough respect on executing it. With such sensitive topic, it needs to be address more sensitive. <br/><br/>At the end, it was Drew who have to come to Fable to rescue her.   <span id="freeText13088252957925253737" style="display:none">So I finally read this book, LOL! Took me long enough. I think it was yesterday? Not sure, I'm on vacation and the days/books are starting to blend together. <br><br>So I'll be honest upfront, I'm not the biggest fan of Monica, her books seem to be more of a hit or miss type deal for me. This was sort of in the middle. In the beginning, I struggled with the writing, found it choppy and kind of disjointed. We were given some mystery surrounding the characters which was nice but nothing to actually connect the reader to them. <br><br>I never exactly cared for Fable but liked her more so in the second half. I really liked her and Drew together and felt like they could be complementary. Drew I definitely hurt for. I couldn't imagine the crap going through his head with what he has had to deal with and the impact and guilt it would have on him. <br><br>Okay, as for the twist/secrets... I kind of guessed the first one (I'm assuming that most people would have so yay me?) but the second is kind of really messed up? Like I was just left with a bad taste in my mouth - again, the authors point, I get but ewwwww. Wtf. That's just badness. I hate the antagonist like a mofo so that's always promising. <br><br>Then I simultaneously love and hate the ending. It's what's the characters needed so I'm glad the author didn't just bullshit everyone at the end but I would've liked a smidgen more coupley-ness to leave with the reader perhaps. <br><br>But damn now I need the next book. And if no one has noticed yet, I don't read series'. I read the first book and then move on because I have book ADD and get way too distracted, but crap on a cracker Monica now I need more of these two! So I'll get around to it......... <div id="review_1074674015" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1074674015" />
    <a title="Ty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30039347-ty"><img alt="Ty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395942069p2/30039347.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1074674015?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ty" href="/user/show/30039347-ty">Ty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30039347-ty?shelf=i-can-t-even">i-can-t-even</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30039347-ty?shelf=no">no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30039347-ty?shelf=walk-it-off">walk-it-off</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30039347-ty?shelf=eh-no">eh-no</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1074674015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer381961004164251993">Oh, my... Am I really going to be the unpopular opinion? I can't believe the amount of five stars this is getting. Is there something wrong with my copy of the book or something? Because I found it infuriatingly ridiculous. It was like reading a bad-written soap opera. Despite all the forced drama that gathered in piles and piles I laughed trough this thing.<br/><br/>And I just kept wondering if the editor of this book hit his head or something. There were so many mistakes: <br/>"The perfection description of </span>
  <span id="freeText381961004164251993" style="display:none">Oh, my... Am I really going to be the unpopular opinion? I can't believe the amount of five stars this is getting. Is there something wrong with my copy of the book or something? Because I found it infuriatingly ridiculous. It was like reading a bad-written soap opera. Despite all the forced drama that gathered in piles and piles I laughed trough this thing.<br /><br />And I just kept wondering if the editor of this book hit his head or something. There were so many mistakes: <br />"The perfection description of how I'm feeling right now" &lt;-This is from page one. PAGE ONE. <br />"No matter how selfish I want I am." <br />"Do you think that less of me?" <br />And so on... A LOT of them.<br /><br />Now, the story... For starters, Fabble (Yes, Fabble) describes herself as a walking, talking cliché more than once. I agree. This whole thing is such a big fat sappy cliché. <br /><br />And the stereotypes. O. M. G. <br /><br />Let's start by jealousy being so hawt. Are you for real? Mad jealousy IS NOT HOT. Tossing things because he found out you were talking on the phone with other guy? NOT COOL. Not to mention that guy being your little brother. But of course, no one shall dare ask. <br /><br />Someone forcefull and possesive? NOT COOL. That sort of relationship is not sane. Putting this sort of macho stereotype out there as the standard example of a hot, great guy is sick. You should not want someone like that in your life. Or should I say "Taking control of your life"? Of course, if this is what you feel you need, that's your own prob. <br /><br />And the barely contained anger? This sort of characters are always so full of it and I'm so tired of this, is this really how you would want your daughter to think? Your sister? Yourself? Letting a guy toss a girl around because he's mad at the world and getting it out on her because, "duh, he needs somewhere to put all that anger" is wrong on so many levels. <br />And then she goes all <b>"Even though he's taking all his anger and turmoil out on me, this has to be good for him, right?"</b> Wrong. He needs therapy, anger control management, and maybe even a hitman to kill his incredibly stupidly clichéd fucked up stepmother, not shake you and barely contain his anger. And you need to run. But of course, doom will come if they are apart for longer than a couple of hours, and if they spend a day withouth some hawt sex, brace yourselfs. UGH.<br /><br />I considered titling this review: "Sex fixes it all." Because that's sort of the message this book sends, yes, I get it, I knew how this book was rated concerning that, but my... it bordered on nonsensical. Bad news, sex. Good news, sex. Someone was sad, sex. Someone was happy, sex. Walk, sex. Talk, sex. Someone dies, sex. Someone cries, sex. UGH. There has to be a limit. Oh, and let's not forget the stereotypical 'physical perfection' of both "perfectly round", "incredibly large", and always so very... skilled. My eye-rolling went to saiyan level thanks to this book.<br /><br />Anyways, I don't really think I need to prove my point further, but let's just finish this up with some lovely quotes.<br /><br /><br />"All those clichés you read about in books and see on TV or movies, that's me. I am a walking cliché." Yes, you are. So is your boyfriend and your entire world.<br /><br /><br />"They literally bat their fake eyelashes at the guys and everything. It's pathetic, what attention whores they are." You are such a charming girl.<br /><br /><br />"Even though whatever she's done with other guys might qualify her as a whore, sex is the farthest thing on my mind when it comes to her." Such a gentleman. And trust me, the no-sex-on-my-mind lasts about three seconds. Tops.<br /><br /><br />"Is there really a possibility he's a virgin? I know they're out there, but I never figured Drew Callahan for one." Oh, get away from that alien race of people. BEWARE! THERE MIGHT BE VIRGINS AROUND! <br /><br /><br />Gah, this was stressing. I think there's nonexisting to none chance of me continuing this series. I can betcha it'll end like Beautiful Disaster. But this was way worse.</span>
  <a data-text-id="381961004164251993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer527086753602499116">01/31/2013 --<br/><br/><b><br/>Overall Rating = 4 Stars<br/>Book Cover / Book Blurb = 3 / 2 = 2.5 Stars<br/>Writer’s Voice = 4 Stars<br/>Character Development = 4 Stars<br/>Story Appreciation = 4 Stars<br/>Worth the Chili = 5 Stars [$3 Amazon & B&N]<br/></b><br/><br/>I have my GoodReads friends to thank for this one. Not even on my radar until I saw a conversation about it. Intrigued right away so bought it. I read it immediately [which doesn't happen often]. I'm very glad I did. It touched on some tough subject content we don't think about often <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spo</a></span>
  <span id="freeText527086753602499116" style="display:none">01/31/2013 --<br /><br /><b><br />Overall Rating = 4 Stars<br />Book Cover / Book Blurb = 3 / 2 = 2.5 Stars<br />Writer’s Voice = 4 Stars<br />Character Development = 4 Stars<br />Story Appreciation = 4 Stars<br />Worth the Chili = 5 Stars [$3 Amazon &amp; B&amp;N]<br /></b><br /><br />I have my GoodReads friends to thank for this one. Not even on my radar until I saw a conversation about it. Intrigued right away so bought it. I read it immediately [which doesn't happen often]. I'm very glad I did. It touched on some tough subject content we don't think about often <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[incest between a son and a stepmother <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />I think the author has a strong voice. I was surprised and very pleased. The only thing I can say I really didn't like, the use of the "cliffhanging" ending. We have another to look forward to, but not sure exactly when. I may not have read it so soon, if I knew I was going to have to wait to see these two fully commit.<br /><br /><u>What things did I really like</u>?<br />1 -- The subject content. The author handled some sensitive topics very well.<br />2 -- The voice of the author -- she does a very nice job. I moved through the story quickly. It isn't short, but it moves well.<br />3 -- The characters. I really liked Drew and Fable [just love this name!].<br /><br /><u>What didn't I like or appreciate</u>?<br />1 -- Not a fan of the cliffhanger ending. Not at all. What is up with this all of a sudden. EVERY FREAKIN' author thinks this is the way to go. We have more series than we can keep up with. SERIOUSLY!! Crazy making.<br />2 -- The blurb put me off. If I hadn't seen some conversation about this book and how good it was, I probably wouldn't have read it based on the cover and the blurb. Neither did much for me. The blurb is in Fable's first person POV. This isn't really how the story is told and if you don't like reading books from this viewpoint, you may not give it a shot. That would be sad because this book is very good.<br />3 -- The cover -- mentioned before. Nothing outstanding, so didn't pull me.<br /><br />Overall, a very good read. I'd recommend this book to anyone wanting a good story with a bit of meat. Not the fluff you think it will be.<br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>

<div id="review_534714531" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/534714531" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/534714531?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite-hotties">favorite-hotties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=alternating-pov-s">alternating-pov-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=male-point-of-view">male-point-of-view</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=contemp-romance">contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>,
