        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer534714531" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6486449231105327656">Fan-fucking-tastic!!!!!! Wow! This book was amazing! I was sucked into Drew and Fable's story from the beginning. Shit, so many secrets and twists my mind was reeling! But damn if I didn't feel heartbroken and happiness all at once. That last part had me crying, from sadness and possibly tears of hope. I can NOT wait for the continuation!! <br/><br/>Full review to come!<br/><br/>This book was all over GR and I was getting curious about it. So what did I do? One Click on Amazon, I did. I'd read some reviews and was </span>
  <span id="freeText6486449231105327656" style="display:none">Fan-fucking-tastic!!!!!! Wow! This book was amazing! I was sucked into Drew and Fable's story from the beginning. Shit, so many secrets and twists my mind was reeling! But damn if I didn't feel heartbroken and happiness all at once. That last part had me crying, from sadness and possibly tears of hope. I can NOT wait for the continuation!! <br><br>Full review to come!<br><br>This book was all over GR and I was getting curious about it. So what did I do? One Click on Amazon, I did. I'd read some reviews and was instantly intrigued. Not to mention that cover, HOT DAMN. That would have anyone wanting to read it. But what was inside was even more beautiful....broken boy with disturbing secrets + broken girl wanting to save said broken boy from his past and you got Drew + Fable. A love story filled with pain, grief, loss and love.<br><br>Drew Callahan is the hot spoiled rich college football star. His life looks perfect on the outside. He's sexy, rich and totally sweet. He could have any girl he wants. Any. Girl. Yet on the inside he's holding onto secrets that are life shattering and shocking to the core and a bit disturbing. Which is why he's not really the dating type. He throws himself into football and school and that's it. But when it comes to the week of Thanksgiving, he asks a girl for help, possibly the only one that could help him and make him forget his real problems. His life is far from perfect.<br><br>Fable Maguire is a barmaid and waitress. She works 2 jobs to help take care of her little brother because their deadbeat alcoholic irresponsible whore of a mother is too damn busy sticking her shit into "other" things than giving a shit about parental roles. She's got her priorities fucked up. So, Fable decides to step up and play mother to Owen, her 13 year brother who's getting into trouble and acting out. But that's normal right for boys his age? Still, Fable grows concerned, especially when she has to leave him at home for a week. Everyone thinks Fable is the town slut because, well she's been around. But she's far from what the rumors are saying. All she's ever wanted to be was loved and wanted. Was that too much to ask? <br><br>Drew approaches Fable after a work night at the bar and asks for her to come home with him for Thanksgiving week. He even pays her. To be his pretend girlfriend. To prove something to his parents. <br><br>And she accepts. What she doesn't plan on is falling for him, all the while learning Drew's deep, dark disturbing secrets that may send her running.<br><br>Or it may be the one thing that brings them together. Who knows?<br><br><br>I loved this book! I devoured it in a day, actually from the time I started it last night and then finished today, it was less than 24 hours. I loved it. I guessed some things that were going to happen but it didn't make it easier when it was revealed. If anything, it made it that much harder. I LOVED the fact that it was from both POV's. That is what initially had me reading this book. I love when books are told from both MC's. And in this case, it was essential. We saw both of their struggles as they both faced difficult choices and emotions that neither were familiar with. The steam was perfect and beyond HOT! Holy hell, Drew had me weak in the knees. He had me glad I wasn't in public at some parts. That boy can make you wet just with his voice. DAMN!!! I loved Drew. I loved his voice and how he felt when he was falling for Fable. For real. Not the fake "you're my girlfriend for a week so we have to pretend" way. No, when he realized that life without her was useless and uncomprehencible. I loved his inner voice. I loved his emotions when they surfaced and we got glimpses of the sweet, vulnerable side and it was sexy as shit. His fears, his doubts, his pain when he we find out about his secrets he's holding so deeply to his heart. It was overwhelming. I felt so bad for him. I wanted to comfort him and tell him it wasn't his fault. I wanted him to know he's better than what he thinks he is and deserves love just like everyone else. He does. I loved him. Drew D. Callahan. Ahhhhhhhh<br><br><br>My Drew:<br><br><a href="http://s981.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Drew_zpsbe1bb5a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409432i/801693._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Drew_zpsbe1bb5a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Fable. She was awesome. Her kind and generous spirit. Wanting to help Drew face his demons and she still stuck around. She didn't run. It was so noble of her. I loved her inner voice as well. The way she was struggling with certain things. Being thrown into such a crazy whirlwind and she stood her ground even though she was scared shitless. I'd say she was a brave, courageous chick. Drew was lucky to have her and vise versa. They both belonged together. Their sexual chemistry was off the charts. The way they described each other. The way they talked about each other's bodies, not like ravenous animals just wanting to fuck like jack rabbits. But they really cared deeply on an emotional level. It was so sweet and beautiful to see them grow together and find love in each other. Neither one expecting anything more than a fake show for the people around them. But here they were, really falling for one another, scared shitless yet determined to show how much they meant to each other. LOVED IT!<br><br>My Fable:<br><br><a href="http://s981.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/HaydenPannettiere_zps60741cd8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409432i/801694.jpg" alt=" photo HaydenPannettiere_zps60741cd8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>My Adele....though she has black hair, I couldn't help but picture Kristen. She's described as beautiful and young, right? I couldn't help but see her. Just picture Kristen with black hair(though I doubt she would look good as anything but a blonde) but oh well. It's just my vision.<br><br> <a href="http://s981.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Adele_zpsffb61aa8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409432i/801695._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Adele_zpsffb61aa8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>“But this girl...she doesn’t feel pointless. She’s real and she’s beautiful and she fits perfectly when she’s in my arms. She makes me want to feel.” -Drew<br><br><br>P.S. M*A*R*S*H*M*A*L*L*O*W....<br><br>I need the next book now, please!!!!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6486449231105327656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer419973741946442597">Drew is a star athlete at his College<br/>Popular<br/>Hot<br/>Rich <br/>Girls want him <br/>Guys want be him <br/><br/>But he has secrets…<br/>Secrets he doesn’t want anyone to know…<br/>He may be rich, hot and popular but no-one really notices that he doesn’t date, or have close friends. <br/>And he doesn’t want to go home for the Thanksgiving break alone. <br/><br/>Fable is a townie <br/>She works in a bar <br/>Doesn’t go to College <br/>Loves her brother <br/>She is known for getting around with the college guys.<br/><br/>But she has secrets<br/>Home life isn’t great,<br/>Is poor<br/>And she doe</span>
  <span id="freeText419973741946442597" style="display:none">Drew is a star athlete at his College<br>Popular<br>Hot<br>Rich <br>Girls want him <br>Guys want be him <br><br>But he has secrets…<br>Secrets he doesn’t want anyone to know…<br>He may be rich, hot and popular but no-one really notices that he doesn’t date, or have close friends. <br>And he doesn’t want to go home for the Thanksgiving break alone. <br><br>Fable is a townie <br>She works in a bar <br>Doesn’t go to College <br>Loves her brother <br>She is known for getting around with the college guys.<br><br>But she has secrets<br>Home life isn’t great,<br>Is poor<br>And she doesn’t get around as much as the rumours say she does <br><br>Drew has heard of Fable from his friends. <br>He offers her a pretty woman proposition. <br>Come home with him for the week, pretend to be his girlfriend and he will pay her $3000<br>He doesn’t want to have sex with her. <br>He just needs her to be there. <br><br>It is a tense week. <br>Drew’s Father is busting his balls about his future. <br>His Step-Mother Adele is just being a plain bitch to Fable and Drew <br>It’s the longest week of their lives, <br><br>Until Drew has a meltdown. <br>It was supposed to push Fable away but it bought them closer. <br>She is helping him more than he knew he needed. <br>She is falling for him more than she should. <br><br>On the final day of there week long “Fake” Relationship <br><br>Just like a house of cards <br>It all comes crashing down <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/houseofcards_zps3aac3656.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405919ra/791352.gif" alt=" photo houseofcards_zps3aac3656.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Everything is revealed…. <br><br>And then of course <br><br><b>A CLIFFHANGER</b> <br><br><b>GAH!!</b> <br>Really??!! Is it because I guessed the secret pretty quickly and figured out Adele was the devil that you just sprung a cliff hanger on me?! <br>I was expecting a nice little HEA but NOOOOO! <br><br>Ok in saying that the cliff hanger is no where near as bad as I have read lately, and it was actually kinda cute but still leaves you with unanswered questions! <br>So yes. <br>I will be reading the second book! . <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="419973741946442597" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_517264167" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/517264167" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/517264167?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17409186-one-week-girlfriend">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=college">college</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer517264167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10464362197336232523">Thank god I waited to read the first book until the second one came out. Otherwise I'd be<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/566031.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> and<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311519ra/688544.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>From the outside, it looks like Drew Callahan has it all; looks, a successful college football career, money. But inside he is harboring a secret so deep and dark, that it rules his entire being turning him into a robot, a shell, unfeeling.<br/><br/>In a desperate attempt to deal with the nightmares that plague him with an upcoming trip to his childhood home for Thanksgiving, he approaches Fable, a girl he doesn't</span>
  <span id="freeText10464362197336232523" style="display:none">Thank god I waited to read the first book until the second one came out. Otherwise I'd be<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/566031.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> and<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311519ra/688544.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the outside, it looks like Drew Callahan has it all; looks, a successful college football career, money. But inside he is harboring a secret so deep and dark, that it rules his entire being turning him into a robot, a shell, unfeeling.<br><br>In a desperate attempt to deal with the nightmares that plague him with an upcoming trip to his childhood home for Thanksgiving, he approaches Fable, a girl he doesn't know but has a reputation that fits his means, with a proposition. He will pay her $3,000 to pretend to be his girldriend for a week and go with him back home.<br><br>Fable is a girl that is dealing with her own demons. She takes care of her 13 year old brother because her mother is an alcoholic. Desperate to make ends meet, she agrees to Drew's proposition.<br><br>In the week that follows, relationships change, feelings grow, and secrets are revealed. And something that was only supposed to be pretend, turns into something very very real.<br><br>This book was an emotional roller coaster for me. Drew is such a tortured soul, it hurt my heart. <br><br>10% into the book I had a feeling about what his secret might be.<br>66% it only got worse<br>and when we finally find out about the whole thing<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/592655.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow! just wow!<br><br>Even though I had a pretty good idea what would happen, it didn't make it any less of a gut-wrenching revelation.<br><br>This book deals with a subject that is not typically touched from quite this angle<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[sexual abuse of a male, minor  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I was enthralled with the story from the very first page and could.not.put.it.down until the last. It was emotional, dark, gritty. The relationship that develops between Drew and Fable didn't seem forced or far fetched- it was beautiful to read.<br><br>An emotionally beautiful story about pain, nightmares, forgiveness, and tragedy.<br><br>Starting the 2nd book right now. Can't wait!<br><br>5 stars<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10464362197336232523" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aJu+WOUvV0opT/DJSarUihTbZC1UDfxD8+PPVRXoyI0qOUmx8SkcsAcHvAJiPCRKHpjseHbDh6GasHMP003LkA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sjnOWrGyDN6GzRyP6M0NGoFlhXGrzs5ub4tGWqGu8yzwmzmzpbRHJKiFUETDW/3aiyYNJIkAtYwG2PoAZwvwMQ==')})
  }
